                today_text: "Trời đẹp",

                today_wind_speed: "12m/s",

        methods: {
            onSelectLocation(e) {
                let el = e.target.innerHTML
                let value = e.target.getAttribute('data-value');
                this.loadWeatherData(value);
            },
            setActiveOption(city_name) {
                let self = this;
                this.provinces.forEach(item => {
                    if (item.code == city_name) {
                        item.active = true;
                    } else {
                        item.active = false;
                    }
                });
            },
            loadWeatherData(city_name,show_noty) {
                let self = this
                let site_path = document.querySelector('[name="site_path"]').getAttribute('content');
                self.setActiveOption(city_name);
                show_noty = show_noty == undefined ? false : show_noty;
                fetch(site_path + '/weather?city_name=' + city_name)
                    .then(
                        function(response) {
                            if (response.status !== 200) {
                                console.log('Looks like there was a problem. Status Code: ' +
                                    response.status);
                                return;
                            }
                            response.json().then(function(jdata) {
                                if (jdata.errCode) {
                                    self.weather_data = jdata.weather_data;
                                } else {
                                    if (show_noty) {
                                        showMessage('Không có dữ liệu');
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    )
                    .catch(function(err) {
                        console.log('Fetch Error: -S',err);
                    });
            }
        },
        mounted() {
            this.loadWeatherData(this.weather_data.city_name);
        },
    });

<script>
    //vue
    var goldprice_block = new Vue({
        el: "#block_goldprice",
        data: {
            markets: [],
            goldprice_data: []
        },
        methods: {
            loadData(show_noty) {
                let self = this
                let site_path = document.querySelector('[name="site_path"]').getAttribute('content');
                site_path = site_path.replace('/en', '');

                show_noty = show_noty == undefined ? false : show_noty;
                fetch(site_path + '/goldprice')
                    .then(
                        function (res) {
                            if (res.status !== 200) {
                                console.log('Looks like there was a problem. Status Code: ' +
                                    res.status);
                                return;
                            }
                            res.json().then(function (jdata) {
                                if (jdata.errCode) {
                                    self.goldprice_data = jdata.goldprice_data;
                                    self.markets = jdata.markets;
                                } else {
                                    if (show_noty) {
                                        showMessage('Không có dữ liệu');
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    )
                    .catch(function (err) {
                        console.log('Fetch Error: -S', err);
                    });
            }
        },
        mounted() {
            this.loadData();
        }
    });
</script></div><div class="box-items"><!-- currency -->

        $(document).ready(function() {
            if($('#slider-home-hot').length) {

                    slidesPerView: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 15,
                    speed: 800,
                    loop: true,
                    autoplay: true,
                    pagination: false,
                    navigation: {
                        nextEl: '.swiper-next',
                        prevEl: '.swiper-prev',
                    },
                    on: {
                        update: function() {
                            if($.browser.desktop) {
                                var target = $('#block-home-latest').data("target");
                                var maxheight = $('#block-home-latest').data("maxheight");
                                var h_header = $('.block-scroll-right .title').length ? $('.block-scroll-right .title').height() + 35 : 15;
                                var h = maxheight != undefined && maxheight > 0 ? maxheight : $(target).height() - h_header;
                                $('#block-home-latest').mCustomScrollbar({
                                    scrollInertia: 300,
                                    autoHideScrollbar: true,
                                    setHeight: h,
                                });
                            }
                        },
                    },
                });
            }
            if($('#block-home-featured').length) {
                new Swiper('#block-home-featured', {
                    slidesPerView: 3,
                    spaceBetween: 15,
                    // slidesPerGroupSkip: 0,
                    loop: false,

                        nextEl: '.swiper-next',
                        prevEl: '.swiper-prev',

                    breakpoints: {
                        320: {
                            slidesPerView: 2,
                            slidesPerGroup: 2
                        },

                            slidesPerGroup: 2
                        },

	<script type="text/javascript">
		$(document).ready(function() {
			function loadSliderCategory(id) {
				var data_slider = JSON.parse('{"item_mobile":2,"item_desktop":5}');
				var autoplay_opt = {
					delay: 2500,
					disableOnInteraction: true,
				};
				var loop = parseInt('1') ? true : false;
				var autoplay = parseInt('1') ? false : false;
				var delay = parseInt('5') * 1000;
				new Swiper(id,{
					loop: loop,
					pagination: false,
					navigation: {
						nextEl: '.swiper-next',
						prevEl: '.swiper-prev',
					},
					autoplay: autoplay,
					breakpoints: {
						320: {
							slidesPerView: data_slider.item_mobile,
							spaceBetween: 15
						},
						480: {
							slidesPerView: data_slider.item_mobile,
							spaceBetween: 15
						},
						1024: {
							slidesPerView: data_slider.item_desktop,
							spaceBetween: 18
						}
					}
				});
			}
			loadSliderCategory('#video')

		});
	</script>
		<script type="text/javascript">
			$(document).ready(function() {
				if ($('#content-slider-52').length) {
					var data_slider = JSON.parse('{"item_mobile":2,"item_desktop":4}');
					var autoplay_opt = {
						delay: 2500,
						disableOnInteraction: true,
					};
					var loop = parseInt('1') ? true : false;
					var autoplay = parseInt('1') ? true : false;
					var delay = parseInt('5') * 1000;
					if (!autoplay) {
						autoplay_opt = false;
					} else {
						autoplay_opt.delay = delay;
					}
					// console.log(loop, autoplay, delay, autoplay_opt);
					new Swiper('#content-slider-52',{
						loop: loop,
						pagination: false,
						navigation: {
							nextEl: '.swiper-next',
							prevEl: '.swiper-prev',
						},
						autoplay: autoplay_opt,
						breakpoints: {
							320: {
								slidesPerView: data_slider.item_mobile,
								spaceBetween: 10
							},
							480: {
								slidesPerView: data_slider.item_mobile,
								spaceBetween: 10
							},
							1024: {
								slidesPerView: data_slider.item_desktop,
								spaceBetween: 10
							}
						}
					});
				}
			});
		</script>
	        <script type="text/javascript">

            $(function() {
                $('#header_search_submit').click(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var keyword = $('#header_search_keyword').val();
                    var exactly = $('#presies').prop('checked');
                    var txt = (exactly == true) ? 'on' : '';
                    if(!(/[\<\>]/).test(keyword)) {
                        location.href = '/search?keyword=' + encodeURI(keyword) + '&chinhxac=' + txt;
                    } else {
                        showMessage('Invalid keyword');
                    }
                });
                $('#header_search_keyword').on('keyup', function(e) {
                    var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
                    if(keycode == 13) {
                        $('#header_search_submit').trigger('click');
                    }
                });
            })
        </script>
            <script>
            function loadWeatherData(city_name) {
                $.ajax({
                    type: "get",
                    url: '/weather?city_name=' + city_name,
                    dataType: "json",
                    loading: false,
                    success: function(res) {
                        try {
                            if (res.errCode) {
                                var forecasts = res.weather_data.forecasts[0];
                                var weather = $('.weather');
                                weather.find('.wtoday').html(res.weather_data.today_temp);
                                weather.find('.wicon').html(res.weather_data.today_icon);
                                weather.find('.wlow').html(forecasts.forecast_low);
                                weather.find('.whigh').html(forecasts.forecast_high);
                            } else {
                                console.log('Không có dữ liệu');
                            }
                        } catch (error) {
                            console.log(error);
                        }
                    },
                    error: function() {
                        if (response.status !== 200) {
                            console.log('Looks like there was a problem. Status Code: ' +
                                response.status);
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            loadWeatherData('tay_ninh');
        </script>
